<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Ave Maria
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Méditation sur le Premier Prélude de Piano de S. Bach (original title)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ja">アヴェ・マリア (グノー)</span>; <span title="ar">آفي ماريا</span>; <span title="th">อาเว มารีอา</span>; <span title="ko">아베 마리아</span>; <span title="ca">Ave Maria (Gounod)</span>; <span class="expandline" title="4 more..."><span title="zh">聖母頌</span>; <span title="fa">آوه ماریا</span>; <span title="zh-cn">圣母颂</span>; <span title="es">Ave María</span></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="th">Ave Maria (Bach/Gounod)</span>; <span title="th">อาเว มารีอา (กูโน)</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Gounod,_Charles" title="Category:Gounod, Charles">Gounod, Charles</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>

<td>CG 89a
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>

</th>

</td></tr>

</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>

<tr>
<th>Piece Style

<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>violin (or cello) and piano (organ, 2nd cello <i>ad lib</i>.)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>As noted in Wikipedia, not to be confused with his later Ave Maria settings for choir or for soprano (or tenor) with organ (published posthumously in 1894 by Lemoine.)
</td></tr></table>
